Even if you wear the most boring socks in the world, you will spend at least a few entertaining minutes in here. < text>
We did the lunch cruise around emerald bay and the views are fantastic and the captain‚Äôs narratives were interesting. A few important notes-  it was way too long to bring kids under 12. They were bored and ended up sleeping through the second half of it so that was a complete waste of money. More importantly- the food is atrocious. Plan to eat a hearty meal beforehand because you‚Äôre basically held captive for three and half hours during lunch time and $22 for literally the worst nachos you can imagine (think less-than movie theater quality, stale chips, cheap store bought  queso, and low grade store bought salsa (Note to owners- Costco has way more authentic  salsa options that are probably less expensive to keep in stock) and no available additions like guacamole or sour cream) and the pizza was $20 for only four tiny slices (enough for one kid, definitely not big enough to share) and only bearable because we were all so hungry. The sandwiches were only OK but much, much better than the previously mentioned items. Overall, I‚Äôd say for the cost of the ticket and the cost of the food, it is definitely not worth it. Especially if you have hungry kids. To the owners- please invest in a professional chef to create an easy menu that has quality food, or cut the prices of the food in half because the quality for the price is simply not justifiable, especially when we aren‚Äôt permitted to bring our own food on board. If the food were better than I would say it was worth the cost of the entire experience. Perhaps just book a shorter trip not focused around lunchtime dining.< /text>

< review>
This cruise ship is not handicap accessible as they claim. My partner is in a wheelchair, and even though I called before getting on the cruise to confirm that there were handicap accessible ways to get on the boat/enjoy most of the activities/use the bathroom, the bathrooms were not accessible at all. Getting physically on to the boat was fine, but getting from the on-ramp area into the first floor cabin was tough. We had to really squeeze the chair through the door to get it in.

From moving chairs to sit at a table was fine, but the bathroom situation was the worst. There were two small single-stall rooms. The men's was completely inaccessible to a wheelchair, and the women's was supposed to be "handicap accessible". I informed the crew that I didn't think that a chair would be able to enter the bathroom and close the door, and they insisted that it would be fine. They asked if we would be able to fold the chair to bring it into the room..... to which I had to explain that my partner cannot use their legs so there is no option to fold the chair because they need to be in the chair when entering. They said that they could have the makeshift solution of keeping a further up door open, blocking view of the women's bathroom, and they could have the kitchen keep the galley door closed to give my partner privacy in case the door didn't close. I still didn't believe the chair would fit so I had my partner try to enter the women's room..... the chair didn't even fit through the door frame. Meaning that this cruise thought it okay for my partner to relieve themselves in a hallway?

So yes, you can board the boat in a wheelchair, but you'd need a bladder of steel during dinner and drinks to survive because the chances that you'd be able to use the bathroom are slim unless you have a child-sized chair. I am most disappointed in the poor expectation setting when I called, and the fact that the onboard crew insisted it would be possible to fit a wheelchair in the bathroom.

On a separate note, the food wasn't good. We rented out the boat and had a prefixes menu with four options. I can confirm that at least 3/4 were bad. The teriyaki salmon had a sauce that was sickeningly sweet. The prime rib seemed tasteless. The Portobello mushroom dish tasted like everything had been marinated in straight balsamic vinegar for days. On  positive note, The views of the lake were fantastic, and if you were able bodied this cruise would be beautiful. But don't come for the food. Come for the views only.<//review>

Awesome cruise! Smooth and relaxing! We had a big group with a number of kids and everyone was very happy. We enjoyed  watching the lake while it was still daylight and then sunset. Plenty of space on board. We didnt have dinner but drinks and icecream were very good. The Captain and crew members are very friendly, courteous and easy-going. Tips: booking online has a fee. So call them to book your reservation to save some money.</text>

<Text>I drove by Express Smog and was in a hurry so I dropped in. I was asked whether I had a coupon or a price that I had seen and I said no. I was then told the price was going to be over $80 for a successful test even though the price they advertise on their website is much lower. I should have had the good sense to say no at that point, but I was in a hurry and my registration was due.

The test machine had technical difficulties and kept aborting the test. The attendant said there was a problem with my car's computer or hardware and offered a free retest if I got it repaired.  It seems to be quite uncommon that a smog shop would demand that you pay when an abort occurs. But the contract covered this case, so I paid the already outrageous sum and left empty-handed.

After spending $55 at my local mechanic for an inspection, they couldn't find anything wrong with my car and since I hadn't had any repair it didn't make sense to go back to the original smog shop. I took the car to a different smog shop and it passed smogged on the first try.

I went back for a refund since there appeared to be no issue with my car but was sadly refused. When I said I would be making this negative review, the attendant called the police and accused me of threatening him and threatening to destroy his business.

When the police came, we explained our sides of the story and the police officer politely informed the man that I was allowed to post reviews online and suggested that he give me a refund if he didn't want that. He still refused.

So I cannot recommend express smog. They overcharged me relative to their advertised price, had (what seems to be) broken equipment, and they call the police on their customers.< /Text>< UserId.>

<Review>I am loathe to give less than three stars unless a business / place / service really lets me down.  Charlie's was on the bubble of getting into 2 1/2 star territory.  I'm giving them the benefit of the doubt as an indy restaurant on a cute street in the historic part of Upland.

Dear Hubby and I were spending the last day of our mini vacation wandering around vintage neighborhoods in Ontario, Upland, and the surrounding areas.  We happened upon the historic district of Upland, parked the car on 2nd Avenue near the gazebo and started walking around.  There were a few antique stores open.  Restaurants were the most plentiful commodity open on a Sunday afternoon.

The striking Americana graphics for Charlie's drew us in.  I was thinking that DH and I would split a deli sandwich and be good to go until dinner time.  My pre-conceived notion of a deli counter with seating wasn't what turned out to be the situation.

Charlie's features a big bar and table seating.  In contrast to the rich wood bar that has seem some stories unfold, I imagine, the dining room is lined with big screen TV's.  The better to watch sports on.  Is it a deli?  Is it a sports bar?  Does the food live up to the beer and wine offerings?  These questions unfolded into semi-satisfactory answers.

What elevated the experience to an okay one was the quality of the hot pastrami sandwich.  The amount of well-seasoned pastrami, paired with lots of dill pickle slices and spicy mustard, sat well on a French roll.  We chose a side salad, though regular fries, sweet potato fries, and other choices also existed as part of the sandwich price.

DH and I have reached the stage where sharing meals at most restaurants is the right amount of food.  Carrying out leftovers while on a trip doesn't usually work out, and wasting food is not a good feeling.  The sandwich and salad were just right for us to share.

One point of downgrade - they had very few options for me as a beverage choice.  I don't drink caffeinated sodas, and don't enjoy sugary drinks, either.  A bar that doesn't have some non-alcoholic options more interesting than something out of the Coke machine doesn't seem like a very creative bar.  Just one woman's opinion.  If we found ourselves in the area again, I'd probably try another establishment over returning to Charlie's.< /Review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOH-Mbfx-Mv1ivt597N4SaIfQRWeB9SaKM_viLh=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNa7_nksgd5wpAAovJi8ksQrkeoLVQacVD263ux=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN5WicUgKoE0nTHPpXojqGUrOPgq0f9aaHLvU-f=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOJvq1IXO5_ZNUHe8o9zlhQ3rlhVDqFTJ90xWYj=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM_8VHmwCWrbYqwytrSerJW85_Ore_CdJcoD2k5=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMpoRuPgr_tloGyKbaM8TxeQ-_Pp1OS1UuX4WAg=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMgoOnxWoPOf8qbEP-h6MJKPMcJtSJ7OGnuaDJZ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics><resp>None</resp><GmapID>0x80c33153f2f3e21b:0x5f8646c3512079e8<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>
